<Review>Highly recommend for COVID testing!! You have to have a video conference with a doctor before you can schedule a COVID test, but there were same day video appointments available, and the call was about 5-7 mins. I needed a rapid test done within the next two days (I completely dropped the ball on scheduling one earlier, so was panicking a little!) The doc was able to get me an appointment for a test the next day in Santa Clara (about 40 mins from me, since the closer clinic was closed on the weekends. But hey, I was fine to drive a little extra if they could get me in on such short notice!). Once the doc ordered the test, I was sent a 2 hour window in which to show up to the clinic for my test. I highly recommend getting there as early as possible in your window (maybe even a little earlier!). The way that the staff handled the drive-up testing was extremely organized and efficient, and everyone was very kind! JUST BE PREPARED TO: 1) wait in a line of cars for a bit, as they move folks into parking spots as earlier cars leave; and 2) wait a little bit more once you are parked (bring some work tO do!) I was in and out in exactly 1 hour, which I will absolutely not complain about. The line looked a little longer as I was leaving, so I imagine the Alesia could be potentially longer than that.
